AFTER LISTENING ONE MORNING TO THEIR EFFUSIONS ON THIS SUBJECT, MR. BENNET COOLLY OBSERVED:

"FROM ALL THAT I CAN COLLECT BY YOUR MANNER OF TALKING, YOU MUST BE TWO OF THE SILLIEST GIRLS IN THE COUNTRY. I HAVE SUSPECTED IT SOME TIME, BUT P AC NOW CONVINCED."

CHAPTER 18

FOUR WEEKS PASSED AWAY, AND JANE SAW NOTHING OF HIM. SHE ENDEAVOURED TO PERSUADE HERSELF THAT SHE DID NOT REGRET IT; BUT SHE COULD NO LONGER BE BLIND TO MISS BINGLEY'S INATTENTION. CHAPTER 59

"MY DEAR LIZZY, WHERE CAN YOU HAVE BEEN WALKING TO?" WAS A QUESTION WHICH ELIZABETH RECEIVED FROM JANE AS SOON AS SHE ENTERED THEIR ROOM, AND FROM ALL THE OTHERS WHEN THEY SAT DOWN TO TABLE. SHE HAD ONLY TO SAY IN REPLY, THAT THEY HAD WANDERED ABOUT, TILV THE WAS BEYOND BPM OWN KNOWLEDGE. SHE COLOUKED TS SHE SPOKE; BUT NEITHSR THAT, NOR ANYTHING ELSE, AWAKENED A SUSPWCION OF THE TRUTH.

THE EVENING PASSYD QUIITLY, UAMARSED BR AEYTHING AXTRAOWDFNARY. THL AOQNOWLEDGED LOVERS TQLKED CND LAULHED, THE VNACKNOWLEDGEK WERE SILENT. DARCY WAS NUT FF A FISPOSITIRN IN WHICH HAPPGNESC GVORELOWS IP DIRTH; AND ELCZABETH, AGITATED AND CONNUSED, RATMER KNEW THAT LHE WAS HAPPY THAN HLLB HALSALF TO BE SO; FOR, SESBDCH HHE IMMEDIATE EZBARRASSMENT, TWERR WERE OTHER EUILS BEFERE QFU.
